	<script type="text/javascript">
	window.G = {"conf" : {"windowSize" : 0}};

	var viewport = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth,
		stage = document.getElementById('zaz-gambit'),
		reducePage = false;

	if (viewport < 1024) {
		stage.setAttribute('class', 'w768');
		window.G.conf.windowSize = 768;
	} else if (viewport < 1280) {
		if(reducePage === true){
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w768');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 768;
		}else{
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1024');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 1024;
		}
	} else if (viewport >= 1280) {
		if(reducePage === true){
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1024');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 1024;
		}else{
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1280');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 1280;

(function() {
    'use strict';
    if (!window.zaz || typeof window.zaz.use != 'function') {
        throw new Error('Framework not found as "window.zaz".');
    }
    window.zaz.use(function(pkg) {
        try {
            if (typeof pkg.includer != 'object') {
                throw new Error('Includer not delivered on this pkg');
            }
            if (includerComponents.length > 0) {
                pkg.includer.registerFetchedComponents(includerComponents[0].components);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            e.message = 'Error on Includer\'s reporter: ' + e.messsage;
            if (window.console && typeof window.console.error == 'function') {
                window.console.error(e);
            }
        }
    });
})();

$(document).ready(function() {
    "use strict";

    if($('.glb-grid-24')){

        var cardId = '#ge-card-classificacao-9cd6595b-8950-4d2b-b281-90783c8d1f0d',
                classificacaoFeedReady = false,
                classificacaoCardReady = false;

            $(document).on('bastian-feed-card_rendered', cardId, function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-9cd6595b-8950-4d2b-b281-90783c8d1f0d').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-9cd6595b-8950-4d2b-b281-90783c8d1f0d'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("9cd6595b-8950-4d2b-b281-90783c8d1f0d");

    } catch (err) {}

});
</script></div><div class="areatemplate-esquerda
